Foreign News

German Representative Proposes Amending the Company Agreement 53

Requests Restriction of Reserve Forces

Ultimately Vetoed by the Preparatory Commission for Disarmament

Geneva, August 8 (National News Agency) The motion submitted by Germany to restrict the reserve forces of the army and navy was vetoed by the Preparatory Commission for Disarmament today. Among the thirty-two countries present, only Germany, China, the Soviet Union, the Netherlands, Sweden, Norway and other six countries voted in favor. France, Italy, Japan, Belgium, Spain and other twelve countries voted against it, while the remaining thirteen countries including Britain, the United States, Canada and other countries abstained from voting. After the results were announced, the German representative stood up and declared that Germany regarded this motion as a touchstone for restricting armaments in the draft disarmament agreement. Now that the result is like this, no further votes will be cast on any amendments to this article. In addition, during the previous discussions, only the Russian representative Litvinov made a speech in favor of the motion. Representatives from France, Japan and Italy strongly opposed it, while the British representative Cecil only spoke briefly and did not take sides.

Geneva, August 8 (Reuters) The Preparatory Commission for Disarmament today rejected the amendment proposed by Germany regarding the first provision of the Disarmament Convention by a vote of twelve to six. This provision stipulates the period of compulsory military service, while the amendment sought to stipulate the number of new recruits each year and the total period of compulsory military service. German representative Bernstorff then declared that this amendment had been abandoned.

Taiwanese Aborigines Use Clever Tactics 54

Raising White Flags to Lure the Enemy

But Ultimately Repelled

Bodies of Hanoka's Troops Discovered

Japanese Aircraft Drop Bombs as a Show of Force

Wushe, September 9 (Teletong) The body of Hanoka Ichiro, who hanged himself in the eastern forest of the Hogo Aboriginal Community, was discovered yesterday. He was wearing formal attire. The aboriginals' tactics are extremely clever. The day before yesterday, they actually raised a white flag and approached the Japanese army. They suddenly launched a surprise attack. The Japanese army was able to repel them because they had machine guns, but it was extremely dangerous. According to captured aboriginals, the tribal chief Manao Rudao quarreled with his wife and ordered her to commit suicide. When his wife refused, he shot her. Yesterday morning at 7:00 AM, Japanese reconnaissance aircraft dropped four bombs into the Masher Creek Valley. The aboriginals emerged from the caves, covered themselves with dead grass, and lay on the small mountains, taking aim at the Japanese expeditionary force.

Bank Run in France 55

Affecting Paris

Public Panic Intensifies

Asterick Bank Granted Judicial Liquidation

Paris, August 8 (National News Agency) Since the Adam Bank suspended payments, panic has intensified among the French people. Rumors have spread, and all banks across the country have experienced runs on deposits. Even the major banks in the capital are not exempt. Today, tens of millions of francs were withdrawn from the Lyons Loan Bank. Three motions for inquiry have been submitted to the National Assembly. Financial leaders are now urging the government to provide prompt relief and are expected to enact legislation to merge Adam Bank with the Northern Loan Bank so that depositors can be repaid in full. Asterick Bank, which closed on Wednesday, is expected to repay 75% of its depositors. Paris, August 8 The Commercial Court today granted judicial liquidation to Asterick Bank after hearing statements from the bank's founders and chairman. The so-called judicial liquidation is an investigation of the bank's assets, debts, and proportional repayment without declaring the bank actually bankrupt.

Austrian Election Fierce 56

Vienna, August 8 (National News Agency) The current Austrian election is one of the most important since the European War. The intensity of propaganda from all parties has never been seen before. Yesterday alone, airplanes, balloons, loudspeakers, and all sorts of imaginable methods were used, leading to very high public emotions. In the evening, many civil police conflicts occurred in various places, and even the deployment of troops was necessary to suppress them. It is still unprecedented in Austrian history for political propaganda to lead to riots. Among the fourteen parties competing in this election, the Social Democratic Party and the middle-class group led by former Prime Minister Schober and the quasi-fascist Heimwehr are the most fiercely competitive. The Heimwehr is confident that it will make a sensation this time like the National Socialist Party of Germany. Its leader, the current Minister of the Interior, Prince Starhemberg, has even repeatedly stated that regardless of the election results, the party will never relinquish political power. Currently, the group is shouting slogans everywhere to overthrow Marxism, while the opposing Social Democratic Party is shouting slogans to overthrow fascism and is confident that it can also win a major victory.

British Cabinet to be Reorganized 57

London, August 8 (National News Agency) British newspapers are commenting on the reorganization of the cabinet, saying that a large part of the Labor Party is dissatisfied with the current cabinet and is demanding reorganization. It is expected that at least three seats will be changed, namely Chancellor of the Exchequer Snowden, First Lord of the Admiralty Alexander, and Secretary of State for India Benn, who are all accused of reactionary tendencies and opposing borrowing to relieve unemployment.

The Political Tide in Germany Comes to an End 58

Tension at the Opening of the National Assembly

The Brüning Government Barely Survives

The National Assembly is Postponed Until Early December

This Winter Will Be an Eventful Season

Special European Correspondent The German political situation after the election and its impact on world politics have already been described in my previous communication. Since the results of the German election were announced, the mood in all European countries has been anxious and unsettled. On the one hand, the internal economic panic in Germany has reached its extreme. Due to fears of sudden changes in the political situation, the financial community has transferred capital to foreign countries to seek safety. Stock market prices have plummeted, and the number of unemployed workers has increased to more than three million. More than 100,000 metal workers have gone on strike because factory owners have proposed wage cuts. The economic impact on politics and the repercussions of political changes have once again affected the economy. This kind of panic scene was only seen once before during the period of the mark's fall in 1923. On the other hand, the victory of the German fascists in the election was like a dream for European countries, who suddenly realized that war was inevitable. Diplomatic conspiracies and competition for armaments have increased without end. The breakdown of the French-Italian naval negotiations, the tense situation in the Balkans, and the increase in France's military budget for the next year were all influenced by the German election to some extent. In this tense situation, what people are hoping for day and night is the question of how the political situation will get through the difficulties after the convocation of the new German National Assembly. The Brüning cabinet has an extremely unstable foothold in the new National Assembly. If the left and right sides jointly attack, it will inevitably fall. But after the fall, into whose hands will German power fall? Will a right-wing cabinet appear, or will the Social Democratic Party reorganize the joint cabinet? Whether it leans to the left or the right is closely related to the international situation in the near future and is what we urgently need to understand.

Now, this first difficult hurdle has been overcome. Although the Brüning cabinet occupies only a minority of seats in the National Assembly, it actually stands firmly without falling. This is something that people did not expect. Since the announcement of the election results, Brüning has exchanged views with the leaders of various parties on the one hand, and has calmly reorganized the financial plan on the other. The most urgent problem for the German government at present is the deficit in the budget. As a result of the stagnation of German industry and commerce in recent months, the national treasury's income has greatly decreased, while the maintenance costs for unemployed workers have increased. Therefore, the budget shortage for this year ranges from 4.5 billion to 6 billion marks, and for the next year, it will be about 1 billion marks. The national treasury is empty and there is no way to raise funds. Any political party forming a government will inevitably feel this difficulty. Brüning advocates economizing on administrative expenses and reducing maintenance costs for unemployed workers. On the other hand, he is borrowing short-term foreign debt from American banking groups in order to make up for it temporarily. After this plan is decided, we will wait quietly for the National Assembly's verdict.

On October 13, the new National Assembly opened. The people were alarmed for a time. Berlin was under intangible martial law throughout the city. One hundred and seven Social Democratic Party members wearing brown uniforms with swastika badges (this kind of uniform is prohibited in Prussia, but there is no way to ban it inside the National Assembly) were clamoring and shouting endlessly in the assembly hall. On the afternoon of that day, many thugs hired by the Social National Party gathered in the commercial area of Berlin and smashed the glass windows of shops opened by Jews (the Social National Party is the most violent against Jews. Hitler said that both capitalism and communism are crimes created by Jews). Many people were arrested by the police before they gradually dispersed. At that time, the people were panicked, as if a revolution was about to break out. On the 15th, when the National Assembly elected the speaker, the left and right factions competed fiercely, but in the end, Luo Bai, a Social Democratic Party member who had served as speaker for many years, was finally elected as speaker. People generally regarded this as a harbinger of the government's victory. On the 16th, the government issued a policy declaration, outlining the current difficulties in Germany and its emergency relief measures, advocating streamlining and reducing administration, and temporarily borrowing foreign debt to meet the current urgent needs. On the other hand, it urged the various parties to temporarily abandon their partisan views and get along with each other for a while in order to get through the crisis. As for foreign affairs, the government advocated using peaceful methods to seek the liberation of the German nation and equal international treatment, but did not advocate taking risks to seek temporary success. This government declaration was praised by the central small parties and the Social Party because of its euphemistic and compromising wording. Therefore, although the debate in the National Assembly on the 17th and 18th was very fierce, the meeting on the 18th did not end until midnight, but the motion of no confidence in the government proposed by the Social National Party, the Communist Party, and other right-wing parties was ultimately voted down by a majority of 318 votes to 236 votes and was not included on the agenda. The National Assembly was postponed until December 3. The financial bills of the Anti-Versailles Treaty proposed by various opposition parties and the amended Young Plan were all submitted to the committee for review. Only the proposal to borrow 125 million marks of short-term foreign debt from foreign banking groups was passed by a majority of 325 votes to 237 votes.

Therefore, the difficult hurdle in the German political situation can be said to have passed temporarily. This is entirely due to the Social Democratic Party's unwillingness to bring down the cabinet at present. The number of votes obtained by the government side in this vote was made up of the Central Party, the People's Party, the Bavarian People's Party, the National Party, and the Economic Party, while the Social Party alone occupied more than 140 votes. As for the opposition parties, in addition to the Social National Party, the Communist Party, and the German National People's Party, which are irreconcilable with the government, only the Farmers' Party joined in. Therefore, the government actually managed to get a majority of 82 votes, which can be said to be fortunate.

The reason why the Social Democratic Party and the central right-leaning parties are making every effort to support the government this time is because the political and economic situation in Germany has become increasingly critical in recent months. If the current government falls, political power will inevitably fall into the hands of the extreme right. If this is the case, the future of the political situation will be unimaginable. Therefore, the various parties are all enduring for the time being so that the current government can safely get through the financial crisis. The Social Democratic Party has made a great sacrifice in this move. The financial bill issued by the Brüning cabinet this time completely represents the interests of the bourgeoisie and is especially harmful to the interests of the workers. It is no different from the Social Party betraying the working class it represents by supporting it, but in order to maintain the remnant of the republic and avoid the dictatorship of the right, it has to adopt this strategy.

But it would be a complete misrepresentation to say that the German political situation will turn from bad to good from now on. The voting in the National Assembly this time was only the first confrontation between the various parties. Although the government managed to win by luck, the current government's policies and the majority of political parties in the National Assembly are mutually exclusive. When the National Assembly reopens in early December, there will inevitably be a more intense debate. The financial and diplomatic cases that are temporarily shelved now will be contested by the various parties based on their own interests. As far as we can see, the Brüning cabinet will have no hope of escaping at that time. If so, the current political tide in Germany is only a ceasefire for more than forty days. What the end will be is still a big mystery.

The only thing that is certain is that although the current government has managed to survive, the general trend of the people's hearts and minds in this election and the direction of German foreign policy will inevitably change and will not be able to follow the established rules of the past few years. The postponement of payments under the Young Plan and the proposal to amend the Treaty of Versailles are almost the unanimous demands of all parties in the National Assembly. The government itself cannot ignore them. On the contrary, the Locarno Treaty and the Franco-German cooperation were the masterpieces of Stresemann and will no longer be heard by the Germans from now on. If this is the case, the tense atmosphere in Europe caused by the German election will not be eased by the temporary passage of the current German cabinet through the crisis.

In short, this winter will be a period to watch. Not only will the German political situation determine its direction of development when the National Assembly reopens in December, but the same is true of the major European countries. Austria is currently holding elections, and the Fascist Party is expected to have a great victory in the next National Assembly. The British Labor government still has a certain lifespan, which will be determined in the next parliament. As for France, the right wing is also gradually rising due to the results of the German election. In addition, the Radical Party is carrying out a vote of no confidence in the cabinet. It can be seen that the political situation in the major European countries will undergo significant changes in February and March. Its impact on the overall international situation will not be a minor event. The mountain rain is about to come, and the wind is filling the building. We will wait and see. (Lu Ji in Paris on October 20)

The United States Recognizes the Brazilian Government 59

Washington, August 8 (Reuters) The United States has fully recognized the new Brazilian government. This news was suddenly announced by Secretary of State Stimson. Before this, the Secretary of State and President Hoover had consulted for a long time and jointly considered detailed reports on the Brazilian political situation. The reason why the State Department took this resolute action was clearly to eliminate the diplomatic ill will caused by the United States' refusal to deal with the Brazilian revolutionary army's military supplies. The State Department also knows that if Britain recognizes the new government first, the United States' good market in Brazil will definitely be endangered. The United Kingdom is the most formidable enemy of the United States in this market.

Complete Resolution of Military and Political Affairs in Fujian 66

Lu Xingbang Appointed Commander of Bandit Suppression in Western Fujian

Four Provincial Committee Members Resumed Duties on the 3rd

Fuzhou Correspondence: Chairman Yang, with the Fourth Plenary Session about to open, in addition to compiling and sending provincial proposals for deliberation, also departed for Beijing at 7:00 AM on the 5th, accompanied by Lin Sen, Zheng Baojing, Xu Xianshi, various provincial committee members, Chen Peikun, Lin Jinan, Jiang Pingfan, He Gonggan, Commander-in-Chief of the Land and Naval Forces Chen Jiliang, Division Commander of the 56th Division Liu Heding, and members of the Provincial Party Steering Committee, all of whom saw him off at the riverbank. The duties of the Chairman of the Provincial Government are temporarily managed by Chen Peikun, and the duties of the Director of the Civil Affairs Department are temporarily managed by Zheng Xiaocheng, the chief secretary of the department. Important matters are reported to Chen Peikun for handling, and military affairs are handled by Chen Jiliang. Lin Zhiyuan was originally scheduled to travel with Yang, but Yang ordered him to consult with Fang Shengtao and Sun Benrong to finalize some unfinished procedures, so he will depart tomorrow morning with Fang Shengtao for Shanghai, then to Beijing. Sun Benrong will remain in the province to negotiate the reorganization of Lu's forces.

Regarding military and political issues in the province, Chairman Yang convened Fang Shengtao and others at the headquarters a few days ago to conduct detailed discussions on matters such as pay, provisions, and defense areas. The entire province will be limited to ten regiments, divided into five brigades, with Qian Yuguang, Xiao Shuxuan, Chen Guohui, Zhang Ziming, and others serving as brigade commanders. The remaining brigade will be decided after Lu's forces have been fully incorporated. However, Lu Fang requested that the remnants of his forces be organized into two brigades and one independent regiment. After further discussion, it was decided that if Lu is willing to repent, he should be allowed to atone for his sins. Although organizing the remnants of his forces into two brigades and one independent regiment is somewhat excessive, if he can make efforts for the Party and the nation, his request may be granted. The following resolutions were passed: (1) Lu Xingbang is appointed as the Commander of the Bandit Suppression Front in Western Fujian. (2) All of Lu Fang's troops will withdraw from Youxi and Yanping, and concentrate in Qingliu and Ninghua. (3) After Lu's troops are concentrated in Qingliu and Ninghua, they will advance towards Western Fujian and eliminate the local bandits in Western Fujian within one month. (4) The defense areas of upstream Yanping and Youxi will be filled by troops dispatched by Liu's division, and Jian'ou and Shaowu will be filled by two brigades from the Land and Naval Forces. (5) The garrison locations of Lu's troops will initially be in Ninghua, Qingliu, and Guihua. Garrison locations will be allocated when the local bandits in Western Fujian are eliminated. (6) For the selection of brigade and regimental commanders for Lu's forces, Lu Xingming is proposed for the first brigade, Zhou Zhiqun is proposed for the second brigade, and Lu Xinming is proposed for the independent regiment. After the resolutions were passed, the entire case was handed over to Lu's representative, Lin Shaoqi, to telegraph Lu Xingbang for compliance. The formal appointment of Lu Xingbang as the Commander of Bandit Suppression in Western Fujian will be announced after being submitted to the central government for approval.

Another report says that when Lu Xingbang returned Zheng Baojing and the other five, he sent his nephew, Lin Shaoqi, who is currently the Chief of the Logistics Department of the Division, to the province with Sun Benrong to surrender to Yang Shuzhuang. After arriving in the province, Lin visited Yang several times and strongly argued that the recent unrest was entirely due to the instigation of Yang Yugu and his group, and requested that Lu be leniently treated. Yang discussed this with Liu Heding, Fang Shengtao, Chen Jiliang, and other generals who advocated suppressing Lu, and decided that since Lu had repented, he should show his sincerity. Lin Shaoqi then stated that Lu was willing to lead his troops to assist in suppressing the communist bandits in Western Fujian to atone for his sins. Yang then temporarily gave Lu the title of Commander of Bandit Suppression in Western Fujian, reorganized his troops into two brigades and one regiment, and transferred them to the Western Fujian Ting Prefecture to take on the task of suppressing the communists. However, because both Lu and Zhou were wanted by the National Government, Yang Shuzhuang requested Chairman Chiang to first revoke the arrest warrants when he went to Beijing, and then the provincial government would announce the appointments. Lu Xingming is currently being held in Zhejiang. It is hoped that he will be released after Yang contacts the National Government. Lin Shaoqi returned to Youxi to report after completing his mission one day after Yang Shuzhuang left the province. Currently, ships traveling between the upstream and the provincial capital have completely resumed, restoring the pre-war state. Furthermore, the telegraph poles between Fuzhou, northern Fujian, and Shanghai, which were cut down by Lu's troops after the outbreak of the war, are also being repaired by the Telecommunications Administration and will be restored soon. The military campaign against Lu in Fujian Province will thus come to an end.

The issue of the resumption of duties of the Provincial Government Committee members Zheng Baojing, Lin Zhiyuan, Xu Xianshi, and Cheng Shikui is still awaiting a reply from the National Government, but no reply has been received to date. Yang Shuzhuang was also eager to go to Beijing and could not wait any longer, so a compromise was reached on the 3rd, and the provincial government ordered the four to temporarily resume their duties. On the 4th, a provincial affairs meeting was convened, with all committee members in attendance, and Zheng Baojing was ordered to return to his position as Secretary-General. More than sixty important matters handled by the provincial government during the ten months since the provincial affairs meeting was suspended on January 6th were presented for separate ratification. The meeting began at 9:00 AM and ended at 4:00 PM. In addition, Zheng Baojing and the other three temporarily proposed a case for the commendation of Chen Naiyuan. Three resolutions were passed: (1) A monument will be built at a suitable location in the provincial capital. (2) The surviving family members will be given generous pensions in one lump sum. (3) Tuition fees will be subsidized for their children until they complete their education. Furthermore, regarding the property of Yang Yugu and Wu Xuan, the masterminds of the January 6th Incident, the Civil Affairs Department was ordered to seal it off together with the Municipal Public Security Bureau. Yang Shuzhuang, having completed the arrangements for the Fujian affair, departed for Beijing on the 5th. (November 6th)

Zhejiang Province Reforms the Name of Land Tax

Implemented as Provincial Tax from the 19th Year 70

The Zhejiang Province land tax has always been征收 according to the chapter. The land tax of one yuan and five jiao is the正税, and the three jiao is the糧捐抵補金. The three yuan is the正税, and the three jiao is the省税. Since the land tax has been划归省税, the previous items are no longer applicable. The Finance Department has重行 修訂 and通令各县遵照. The令文云查各县征收田赋向章地丁 one yuan and five jiao as正税, three jiao as糧捐抵補金, three yuan as正税, three jiao as省税 is a system inherited from before the划分 of 国省两税. Since田赋 has been划归省税, the previous items are no longer applicable. This year, Zhejiang Province公布征收地丁抵補金章程 has separately修正 the地丁銀, with each两以 one yuan and eight jiao as the正税 and the抵補金, with each石以 three yuan and three jiao as the正税. The 省税 items under the原有地丁项下 and the三角糧捐抵補金项下 must自十九年份新糧起 be取消一律 to comply with the legal system. In the future, each县报解地丁抵補金 of nineteen年份 shall按 one yuan and eight jiao and three yuan and three jiao列款分解统称 as the正税, and must not再列粮捐省税名目. 其各县在这个通令以前已解粮捐省税 of nineteen年份 will be查明 by the厅 and改收 as正税,用昭劃一. However, the 粮捐 under the 盐税项下 should still be专门报解 and is not included in this limit. 地丁抵補金 of the previous十八年份 should also follow旧贯按正省税粮捐 and is报解分款以清年限. In addition to sending this令separately,合行令仰该县长 and immediately遵照办理.

Jingdezhen Captured by Bandits Three Times

Porcelain Industry Completely Shut Down 71

Total Losses in the Town Reach Tens of Millions

Its commercial prosperity and important position surpass those of other counties in Jiangxi. On the morning of July 6th, communist bandits led by Fang Zhimin from Leping suddenly drove straight into the town with hundreds of bandits. The county police, due to lax defenses, had more than 300 guns confiscated. Fang immediately established a伪 Soviet government. Tens of thousands of workers in Jingzhen, all with shallow knowledge and easily susceptible to bandits'麻醉, immediately formed a general工会. The communist bandits also instigated the workers to arbitrarily抢夺勒令 stores to donate款没收庆泰典铺, and killed巿黨監委, causing panic among the people. Later, it was heard that省军 was about to莅镇, and Fang匪 withdrew on the night of the 9th, but the losses to local shops amounted to more than three million. On the 17th, the省府委派张团长 to the town, and the people's hearts were slightly settled. However, after a few days, the团奉令 returned to省. On September 8th,邵匪式平周匪建屏又乘虚窜至 from Hukou, numbering thousands of bandits, resulting in the second陷落 of Jingzhen. When the匪共入镇, they鸣枪示威. The people heard the sound and were失措, and the shops closed their doors one after another. After the匪入镇, they established a Soviet government at the县府委任磁工詹锦坤 as the General 工会常委. The general亡命工人流氓地痞莫不趨之若鶩, and羣起加入. In less than half a day, more than a hundred大大小小工会 were established, and a大举掠劫 was carried out. Those at the通关要隘 were daily派匪兵看守, traffic was断绝, and the people欲逃不得. The匪徒鸣锣令 ordered the shops to一律开市 within two hours, otherwise they would be没收. The商民 were抵抗无力 and祇得开门. Then the匪 immediately ordered the workers to實行暴动,携带刀枪武器 to each商铺 to search for资本, and then绑去千余人 to龙珠阁 to be用粗蔴绳綑绑 and then用尖刀刺颈. The杀人 as hemp,屍横遍野,诚属惨无人道. Later, it was heard that the谭道源部岳旅 was about to 来景镇. The匪遂于21日逸去, and when臨行时, the former商会会长陈仲西 and在会办事人员二十余人,另肉票数十人, were掳去 and索赎十万元. The statistic景镇loss was no less than five million. The乃岳旅驻镇仅一日 and奉令 returned to省, and the匪徒 then于10月2日捲士重来, numbering more than ten thousand. The people were惊弓之鸟, and闻风丧胆. When the匪 had not抵境, the 先行隻身逃亡者 was not计其数. The 匪共三次到镇 was赤焰较前尤炽. In addition to设立工会, they成立农民协会 and指令农民工人 to use千余辆车 to搬运货物 to各商店. All大大小小商店 and 人民住宅 were被抢夺殆尽,十室十空. Those在逃者 were mostly赤身裸足,栖身无所,家破人亡. Those who were未逃者 were勒入工会, and if there was违抗, they were immediately处死,致使良民亦被迫为匪. To date, the匪共 has盘踞 for more than twenty days and has not退. The瓷厂 has停顿, and the商业 has亦伤. In summary, the三次损失约达数千余万, and the fame of 中外素称瓷产之名区 is恐从兹不易复振,誠 is空前未有之浩劫. (October 24th)

Villagers of Longjing Come to Shenyang to Petition 72

Shenyang Correspondence: Since the conflict between Chinese and Japanese military police in Longjing Village, Yanbian, the situation has become increasingly serious recently. At noon on the 3rd of this month, Fu Qiyang, the supervisor of the Daxing Electric Light Company in Longjing Village, came to Shenyang on behalf of the local people to request assistance from the National Diplomacy Association. According to Fu's account, the market has been extremely panicked since this case occurred. Initially, there were 400 Japanese police officers in various counties in Yanbian, setting up posts along the streets and alleys in Longjing Village. Recently, the number has increased to 800, and they are checking pedestrians at night, causing the merchants and residents to be shocked several times a night. The local officials fear that accidents will occur again, and the Japanese have repeatedly sought to cause provocation, so they ordered the military police not to enter the streets. Fortunately, no further accidents have occurred. This trip to Shenyang is purely to request the support of the people of Liaoning and the Diplomacy Association and to telegram the National Government to lodge a serious protest with the Japanese side so that the people of Yanbian can rest easy. It is闻 that after the Diplomacy Association received Fu's report, it telegraphed the Nanjing Foreign Ministry to seriously negotiate the Longjing Village incident so that the people of Yanbian could安枕. (November 4th)

After the Four-Way Joint Transportation

Eastern Province Tries Out the Beilong Through Train 73

Directly From Beiping to Heilongjiang

Shenyang Correspondence: Since the successful joint transportation of the Northeast Four Routes by the Beining Railway, it has been planned to operate the Northeast-West Four Routes in joint transportation. The vehicles used are still prepared by the Beining Railway, with six sets of undercarriages prepared for daily operation. A trial run has been carried out recently. Because the hooks of the passenger cars are different from the hook dimensions of the Taoang and other railways, it is inconvenient to replace them. The Beining Railway Bureau has ordered the Tangshan Machine Factory to speed up the transformation, and it will be put into operation after the transformation. It is expected to be realized in November. The train is called the Beilong Through Train, and the route passes through the Beining, Sitao, Taoang, and Qike Railways. The travel time is about 41 hours. Major stations include Tongliao, Zhengjiatun, Taonan, Angangxi, etc., directly reaching Qiqihar, the capital of Heilongjiang Province, which is extremely convenient for passengers. The Northeast authorities have long had a plan to form a railway network with the Beining as the center. Now that the Pingji and Beilong through trains have been opened one after another, this plan can be initially completed. It is闻 that the timetable for the Beilong through train has been agreed upon by the Beining and other four railway bureaus. However, the method of the through train is different from that of the Pingji through train. The through train vehicles are attached to the original passenger cars of each road and then operate, so the vehicle numbers used on each road are not uniform. The attached train schedule is as follows:

(1) Beiping to Longjiang (Beining Railway) Train No. 105 departs from Beiping at 11:10 AM and arrives at Dahushan at 6:06 AM. Train No. 703 departs from Dahushan at 7:40 AM and arrives at Tongliao at 6:10 PM. (Sitao Railway) Train No. 8 departs from Tongliao at 7:50 PM and arrives at Zhengjiatun at 11:40 PM. Train No. 3 departs from Zhengjiatun at 0:25 AM and arrives at Taonan at 7:30 AM. (Taoang Qike Railway) Train No. 1 departs from Taonan at 8:40 AM and arrives at Longjiang at 4:55 PM.

(2) Longjiang to Beiping (Taoang Qike Railway) Train No. 2 departs from Longjiang at 8:10 AM and arrives at Taonan at 4:20 PM. (Sitao Railway) Train No. 4 departs from Taonan at 5:45 PM and arrives at Zhengjiatun at 1:40 AM. Train No. 7 departs from Zhengjiatun at 2:10 AM and arrives at Tongliao at 6:00 AM. (Beining Railway) Train No. 704 departs from Tongliao at 7:10 AM and arrives at Dahushan at 5:58 PM. Train No. 106 departs from Dahushan at 6:30 PM and arrives at Beiping at 2:15 PM. (November 4th)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 74

Water Police Captain Rewards Bandit Suppression The first squad leader of the first district of the Provincial Public Security Water Police team, Fan Guozhong, has dispatched detectives to secretly investigate since the township of Lüxiang, under his jurisdiction, was robbed by bandits. He has also instructed the different squads to pay more attention to their assigned areas. In the recent days, he has captured a ringleader, Mo Sifa, with two long rifles and one pistol. The rifle was engraved with characters that stated they were from Zhejiang. He also captured Yang Aqi, who confessed that he followed the group of Taibao Ashu and had bullet wounds on his thumbs and index fingers. He also captured a gang member from Chaohu called Song Fushou, along with firearms. The squad leader was rewarded for being effective in bandit suppression.

Caohejing Prison Inmates are Transferred A group of twenty inmates was transferred from Shanghai to the county for incarceration by policemen dispatched by the Shanghai court. Zhang, the warden, heard of the riots and has requested not to have the inmates transfer to the local dilapidated and crowded facility.

Wuxi 75

Kidnapping Case in Lianrong Town: Ransom Victims Escape Danger. It is already reported in this newspaper that on the evening of the 6th, the home of Hua Jinhan, a wealthy household in the Dongjie of Beiqi Fang, Lianrong Town (Qingcheng City), 15th District, was robbed and Hua's concubine, Ms. Wu, and his eldest daughter, Xiangying, were kidnapped, with a ransom of 20,000 yuan demanded. It is now learned that on the night of the incident, the robbers kidnapped Hua's concubine, Ms. Wu, and Hua Xiangying. They covered the eyes of each of them with black cloth, carried them to Zhangcunbang, and forced them into a bandit boat. The boat sailed to the vicinity of Huangqiao, Jiangyin County, more than ten miles away from Beiqi Fang, and stopped. The bandits removed the black cloth covering their eyes and ordered them to disembark to a dilapidated house. The house consisted of three rooms with a single entrance. Inside, there were straw mats and a few worn-out items. The bandits cooked dinner and offered it to the two ransom victims. After dinner, it was already late at night, and they waited until dawn. The next day (the 7th), one of the bandits, who resembled a ringleader (some say it was an old woman), suddenly said to Ms. Wu and her daughter, "Today, we have decided to send you two home. However, the Tiandan stolen from your home (calculated to be 320 mu, which Hua Jinhan gave to his concubine and daughter in half) must remain here. Your family must prepare the ransom to redeem it. After you return home, do not publicize it. If you report it to the authorities for investigation or fail to redeem the Tiandan, we will send people to set fire to your houses within a short period of time." They then sent bandits to escort Ms. Hua and her daughter to the riverbank, where they boarded a boat and sent them back. At about 8 o'clock that evening, the boat arrived at Xiehe, a place bordering Wuxi (about three miles from Beiqi Fang). They ordered the two to disembark and return home. Ms. Hua and her daughter, because it was already dark, did not recognize the way and wandered for a long time. Later, a fishing boat passed by, and they immediately hired the boat to return home quickly. After arriving home, Hua Jinhan and his son and relatives were overjoyed. Ms. Wu of the Hua family said that one of the robbers in the case had a pockmarked face and looked familiar.

Page 8

It resembled a certain Jia who frequently entered and exited the Xun family. Moreover, the accents of the robbers were all from Jiangyin, so there were clues to be found.

Murder Case: Clues Obtained. It is learned that Zeng Haishan, a local merchant residing at No. 12 Junzi Workshop, Beiqi Kou, in the county, and his concubine, Yao Laoer, were living upstairs when they were suddenly attacked by thugs with knives the night before last, suffering more than twenty wounds to the head, face, hands, ears, and other parts. Afterward, they were admitted to the Brothers Hospital for treatment. It is now learned that Zeng Haishan's condition gradually improved yesterday, but he still could not eat. His first wife, Ms. Zhang, received the news from Suzhou and returned to Wuxi to visit the hospital. She also learned that Yao Laoer was suspected of knowing about the attempted murder of Zeng. Ms. Zhang reported this to the Sixth Sub-Bureau of Public Security in charge and requested that Yao Laoer be arrested. Sub-Bureau Chief Duan, after receiving the report, immediately dispatched police to arrest Yao Laoer and brought her to the bureau for interrogation. She was then transferred to the County Government for questioning.

Shen Yaozu Induces and Abducts Four Female Workers. Shen Yaozu, a young owner of a tofu shop outside the South Gate of the county, is currently working as a clerk in the Yongyu Silk Factory in Yangyao. He is naturally cunning and fond of seeking pleasure. Usually, he specializes in seeking out women, and it is unknown how many respectable girls have been defiled by him. On the afternoon of the 31st of last month, he induced four female workers from the factory, Yu Axin (18 years old), Zhu Aer (19 years old), Feng Hongying (20 years old), and Lu Hexiu (18 years old), to take a car to Shanghai and spend a sweet time together in a rented room. However, the good dream did not last long. Feng Hongying's husband, Feng Wenwei, found out and was very angry. He immediately negotiated with Shen. Shen, realizing that things were not good, returned to Wuxi with Feng Hongying and Lu Hexiu the day before yesterday and stayed at the Railway Hotel. Feng Wenwei also tracked them to Wuxi and reported to the Sixth Sub-Bureau of Public Security. Sub-Bureau Chief Duan, after receiving the report, dispatched police to the Railway Hotel and arrested Shen Yaozu, Feng Hongying, and Lu Hexiu. At the same time, the families of Yu and Zhu heard that their daughters had been induced and abducted to Shanghai by Shen Yaozu and had not returned, fearing that they had been trafficked. Yesterday, they also reported to the Sixth Sub-Bureau and requested an investigation. Sub-Bureau Chief Duan, considering that the case involved inducement, abduction, and trafficking, immediately prepared a document and submitted it to the Main Bureau for transfer to the County Government for handling.

Changzhou 76

Anti-Smuggling Team Headquarters Relocates to Zhenjiang. The Jiangsu Provincial Anti-Smuggling Bureau, due to the impact of smuggled salt on the sales of local salt during the winter season, specifically ordered Pan Jiacai, the commander of the Eighth Anti-Smuggling Brigade stationed in Changzhou, to move the brigade headquarters to Zhenjiang to prevent salt smugglers from entering along the river. Commander Pan, after receiving the order, is preparing to depart. A patrol team will be left in Changzhou to be responsible for anti-smuggling matters.

Kidnappers Abduct Someone Near Dongqing. On the night of the 7th, nine kidnappers suddenly came to the home of Lin Canquan, a farmer near Dongqing in the Fifth District of Wuyi. Each of them carried flashlights and firearms. They entered the house and kidnapped his fourteen-year-old son, demanding a ransom of 600 yuan within a limited time.

Zheng Chengyuan Case Transferred to the Court. Zheng Chengyuan, the former magistrate of Liyang County, Pan Ban, the director of the Finance Bureau, Ren Shuchun, the director of the Education Bureau, Di Hongxun, the chief of the General Affairs Section, Zhou Shi, the director of the Land Tax, Shen Zhiqing, the director of the Record Book, Huang Jian and Cao Qingzhi, the debt collectors, Shi Taoming, a member of the County Party Department, Shi Qinglian and Hu Jinghua, eleven officials in total, who were involved in grain fraud, were detained in the provincial government for a long time. Yesterday afternoon, Chairman Ye sent a platoon of guards to transfer them to the Zhenjiang Court Procuratorate for investigation. Yingchang Match Factory Goes on Strike. In April of this year, the workers of the Zhenjiang Yingchang Factory of the Great China Match Company went on strike once to support the workers of the Shanghai First and Second Factories in their request for retirement pay. Now that the Shanghai factory workers' request has been rejected by the Municipal Arbitration Council and the Shanghai factory has implemented a strike, the Zhenjiang factory heard the news and convened a meeting of all workers at 10:00 AM on the 8th. They decided to go on strike to provide support. The County Federation of Labor immediately summoned the members of the labor union for a discussion and advised them to stop, but to no avail. It also reported the situation to the Provincial and County Party Departments. It has now been ordered to resume work immediately, and the unrest is unlikely to spread.

Construction Bureau Urges Restoration of the Chengtong Northern Section Roadbed. Paramour Conflict Leads to Murder. Fu, the wife of the late Yu Shaoting of Xizi Anchang, Xibao, Beiwai Zha, has been cohabiting with Sun Yehong (from Jiangxi), the squad leader of the Third Company of the First Battalion of the Provincial Security Corps, since her husband's death. Later, she became involved with Qiaosheng, the young owner of Xue Xiangyuan's Western Iron Shop on Beiwai Street. The night before last (the 7th), Sun Yehong's clothes were pawned by Xue Qiaosheng, leading to a conflict. The two grabbed and twisted each other, and Qiaosheng angrily jumped into the river and died. Afterward, Qiaosheng's father, Quan Da, reported to the First Sub-Bureau of Public Security, who dispatched police to detain Sun Yehong. They also reported to the Main Bureau for transfer to the County Government. Yesterday (the 8th) at 4:00 PM, Judge Yang and Inspector Cao went to Xizi Anchang, Beiwai, to conduct an autopsy, bringing Fu's mother, Ms. Wang, her son, A Zhong, and the murderer, Sun Yehong, to the scene.

Gaoyou 80

Kidnapping Case in Nansong Village. The night before last, six bandits in plain clothes, each carrying firearms, suddenly came to Nansong Village in the county. They first went to the home of farmer Ge Cailin and tied up Ge and his wife. They used fire to burn them and tortured them to reveal the location of their hidden silver. Ge cried out in pain and revealed everything. It is reported that clothes and silver dollars were stolen, causing great losses. Afterward, they went to the homes of Tang Yonggao and Song Shangpin, where they searched extensively. Before leaving, they left two threatening letters, one demanding 15,000 yuan from the village and the other demanding 20,000 yuan from the nearby Lin Family Village. Both were required to be delivered to Baoping An on the 19th day of the lunar ninth month. They threatened to set fire and leave no survivors if they were late. The residents of both villages are now uneasy. Those with assets are moving to the city. It is reported that the County Government has ordered the police brigade to send a team to station there for defense.

Nantong 81

All Sectors Express Opinions on the Handling of Banditry Cases by the Court. On the 8th, the district chiefs of all eighteen districts in Nantong County and representatives of various groups and organizations jointly telegraphed the Provincial Government, stating that Nantong County had repeatedly suffered from the disasters of communist bandits killing, plundering, and burning. Fortunately, the provincial and county police and the security regiment cooperated in suppressing and suppressing them, which brought a little peace. However, the communist bandits captured alive and sent to the court were often given lenient sentences based on one-sided statements. Communist bandits who were killed on the spot or attempted to escape were often buried, and the court often granted the requests of their families without first investigating. On the contrary, the teams and regiments that suppressed the bandits were often blamed for this. The bandits became more rampant, and the people became more fearful.

They earnestly requested that the High Court be consulted to strictly order the County Court to pay strict attention to uphold justice and maintain local stability.

Crackdown on Counterfeit Money Selling Organization. A large amount of counterfeit money was discovered in Jinsha District. The main culprit, Zhang Shunyuan, has been arrested. The counterfeit currency amounted to 200,000 yuan. Jinsha is the general distribution center for Jiangbei. The witnesses and evidence have been sent to the County Court for questioning.

Arrest of Murderer at the Morgue. Zhang Jinsheng and Wang Jinsheng, both 17 years old, workers in the fine yarn room of Dasheng Deputy Factory in Chengnan, were laughing with each other when Wang Jinsheng laughed loudly, resulting in Zhang Jinsheng injuring Wang Jinsheng in the waist with a wooden leg, causing him to die. The County Court Prosecutor Zhu went to examine the body and, because the injury was not critical, did not fill out an injury report, causing a great uproar among the local people, women, and children. As a result, a re-examination was conducted and a report was filled out. The prosecutor's office has arrested the murderer, Wang Jinsheng, and the coffin has not yet been nailed shut, as there are still questions.

Huzhou 82

Banditry Cases Occur Frequently in the Western Countryside. The rampant banditry in the Changxing County border of Huzhou is unparalleled. Recently, there have been frequent kidnappings and robberies near the outer city. Ai Qilong, a tenant farmer from outside the Changxing West Gate, relies on farming for a living. Unexpectedly, at about 6:00 PM on the 6th, seven or eight bandits speaking with a Henan accent suddenly broke into his house, ransacked everything, and kidnapped Ai Qilong's daughter, leaving a letter demanding a large sum of money. Furthermore, the family of Chen Xixing, a resident of Qiliting outside the West Gate, was well-to-do. Seeing the rampant banditry in recent years, they moved to the city last year, leaving only workers in the countryside. Unexpectedly, at about 7:00 PM on the 5th of this month, seven bandits with Henan accents, each carrying a wooden-cased gun, rushed to their house, placed a letter of extortion on the table in the middle hall, and fired several shots into the air. The workers in the house had already fled. The bandits entered the house and, finding nothing to take, set fire to Chen's straw pile in the rice field. It is now reported that the extortion letter demanded 26,000 yuan.

Hangzhou 83

Population Survey of Hangzhou City. In recent years, the population of Hangzhou City has been increasing day by day, and prices have also been rising accordingly. However, the most obvious is the price of housing, which has increased more than five times since the founding of the Republic of China. It is unknown how the life of Hangzhou City will change in ten years. The accurate figures recently obtained by the Public Security Bureau are recorded below. The city has a total of 97,316 households, with 301,678 males and 194,938 females, for a total of 496,616 people. This is an increase of more than 2,000 people compared to the previous survey. The number of births is 488, and the mortality rate is 685.

Handling Food Inspection and Registration. The Municipal Government received an order from the Provincial Government yesterday to issue regulations for the inspection and registration of rice entering, exiting, and transiting. According to Article 1, Hangzhou City also has a customs port and should establish an agency to handle the matter so that the central government can statistically analyze surpluses and deficits and allocate resources appropriately. Mayor Cai believes that the matter concerns the ministry's order and that establishing a separate agency for civilian food will incur unnecessary expenses and cause difficulties in implementation. He specifically ordered the departments to comply and establish the agency as soon as possible.

Wei Beitao Suffers from Nerve Disorder in Prison. Wei Beitao, the former chief of the First Section of the Finance Department, was dismissed by the Provincial Government and handed over to the Hangzhou County Local Court for trial on charges of accepting bribes in the Jiasu Shaxian donation case. He was sentenced to five years in prison but appealed. He was detained in the detention center. Recently, Wei suddenly suffered from a nerve disorder, similar to Zhu Zhijue's words. The case was originally scheduled to be continued yesterday (the 9th) by the First Criminal Court. After receiving the report, a forensic doctor was ordered to diagnose and treat him, and it seems difficult to question him for the time being.

Ningbo 84

Ningbo City Continues to Exist. The village and neighborhood committees and citizens of Ningbo City believe that since the establishment of Ningbo City more than three years ago, it has wasted more than 2 million yuan of public funds and has achieved nothing. The gains do not outweigh the losses. Moreover, the population of Ningbo City is less than 200,000, which is not in line with the regulations for organizing a city government. They have repeatedly petitioned the Provincial Government and forwarded it to the Central Government, requesting the abolition of Ningbo City in order to reduce the burden on the citizens. In the past three or four months, they have loudly called for this movement. After Chairman Chiang returned to Fenghua, the various committees and citizens also elected representatives twice to go to Fenghua and submit petitions to Chairman Chiang. It is now learned that the National Government decided yesterday that Ningbo City should continue to be established due to its special historical relationship. The outcry to abolish the city will gradually subside.

Pirates Invade Ligang for the Second Time. More than ninety pirates, on the 30th of last month, seeing that there was no news of a ransom for the kidnapped victims and that the Haijing warship sent to the area by the Water Police Bureau had left, banded together again with seventy or eighty people and went to Ligang on the afternoon of the 4th to intimidate and demonstrate. The residents fled again upon hearing the news, and no one dared to stay overnight. Mr. Wang and other gentry in the village, believing that the livelihood of the people would be unbearable in the long run, jointly went to the city yesterday to request troops to be stationed there.

Fire in Xiaoyao Hang Burns Down More Than Forty Homes. Yesterday afternoon at about 5:00 PM, a fire suddenly broke out in the home of resident Shen Weiyao in Xiaoyao Hang, Dongcang Village, Yinzhou West. The area is located in a remote mountain area with no firefighting equipment. The fire burned for two hours before it was extinguished. It is estimated that 44 families, including those of Shen Libing and Shen Mei, were affected, and 68 houses of all sizes were burned. It is reported that the affected households all rely on firewood cutting and bamboo planting for a living. They all wailed in grief after suffering this disaster.

The Ministry of Education Does Not Allow Winter Vacation Again 87

The Central News Agency reported that the Ministry of Education recently issued an order to all levels of schools across the country prohibiting them from having winter vacations again. The original order is recorded below:

It has been found that the winter vacation for schools is actually a disguised form of the lunar New Year holiday. The Ministry has previously followed the National Government's repeated promotion of the national calendar and the prohibition of the lunar calendar, and has decided to abolish it. Since the 19th year, all levels of schools across the country must not have winter vacations again. The date of the national New Year holiday has been extended to three weeks. The regulations on the school year, semester, and holiday dates have been revised and submitted to the National Government for approval and filing, and an order was issued on March 22 of this year to all for compliance. Now that the date of the national New Year holiday is approaching, the Ministry is deeply concerned that at the beginning of the reform, schools may be insincere in their compliance. It is reiterated that since the 19th year, all levels of schools across the country, except for Guangdong Province, which is allowed to reduce the New Year holiday by one week and move it to the summer vacation due to its proximity to the tropics, should strictly comply with the revised regulations on the school year, semester, and holiday dates and have a three-week national New Year holiday. They must not have winter vacations outside of the national New Year holiday, and they must not reduce the number of New Year holiday days without authorization or exceed the restrictions on the number of days for the start of the semester and arbitrarily increase the number of days for disguised winter vacations in order to comply with the purpose of promoting the national calendar. You are hereby instructed to comply and instruct your subordinates to comply with this order.

Suzhou Agricultural School Announces the Course of the Disturbance

Pan Tianjue, Director of Training, Is Indeed Suspected of Instigating It 88

The Suzhou Agricultural School, regarding the disturbance among pre-college students, issued a statement to all sectors: The school was unfortunately involved in a disturbance by a small number of pre-college students on October 31, who used the reason that the porridge contained bean husks to beat teachers and hold them hostage for a strike. The beginning and end of the situation are hereby presented to all sectors. After the school was reorganized in the 16th year of the Republic of China and the academic atmosphere was rampant, it followed the party's program and made a decision to implement strict training. Therefore, in order to implement strict training, the pre-college students should be taught in separate schools so that they can be given appropriate training separately. Therefore, in the summer of the 17th year of the Republic of China, the pre-college students were separately set up in Liuyuan Road to strictly train the party.

Illegal Meeting of the Student Union 89

The dispute over the principal issue has now been resolved. The University Student Union, citing Liu Shichao and others' violation of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's "Preliminary of People's Rights" by arbitrarily implementing illegal proposals after a quorum shortage at the general assembly, had petitioned the Beijing Municipal Party Headquarters to prevent it. Now, Beijing Municipal Party Headquarters' Twelfth Approval states: "Received the petition, and after investigation, this headquarters also received a petition from the Eighth District Executive Committee. This headquarters' 66th meeting resolved that the student union's assembly had not been reported to this headquarters in accordance with the law, and the establishment of a special committee is particularly inappropriate. In addition to ordering the Eighth District Reporting Committee, you are hereby notified."

Mr. Dai Qixiang is requested to be the director, taking full responsibility for all pre-college professors. For three years, the academic atmosphere has been orderly, and students have greatly admired and harmoniously coexisted with Mr. Dai without any conflicts. This demonstrates that Mr. Dai's management of the pre-college program is appropriately strict and lenient. This semester, because Mr. Dai's teaching hours are relatively numerous and his duties in the academic affairs are heavy, the newly appointed Dean of Students and Party Ideology teacher, Pan Tianjue, will be stationed at the Second Academy as a fundamental training measure, taking full responsibility for discipline and dormitory affairs. For the convenience of operation, Li Fengming was introduced by Mr. Pan as the dormitory staff member of the Second Academy. Only two months after taking office, Mr. Pan was deemed too irresponsible in terms of management and discipline, and students were entering and leaving freely, violating the school's regulations. Therefore, the school principal instructed Mr. Pan to transfer to the First Academy on November 1st. Unexpectedly, on the morning of the 31st, students used the pretext that there were bean shells mixed in the porridge, smashed dozens of bowls, and without asking about the situation, swarmed into Director Dai's bedroom, severely beating him and driving him out of the school, locking the main gate. Other teachers, hearing the alarm, gathered and saw that Mr. Dai was not fully dressed and had suffered many injuries. They immediately called for medical treatment and gathered for a lecture, earnestly admonishing and instructing them to attend classes as usual. Most students expressed acceptance, but a few students obstructed them, creating a wait-and-see situation. In less than half an hour, declarations and slogans had spread throughout the school. The order of the dining hall and the quality of the food are the responsibility of the Dean of Students and the dormitory staff. It is suspicious that students did not inquire of Mr. Pan and Mr. Li, but instead made a scene with Mr. Dai. Moreover, when students swarmed to Mr. Dai's residence, it was 6:15 in the morning, only fifteen minutes after the wake-up bell, and before breakfast time, students took action. Therefore, most students did not eat breakfast that day. After the upheaval broke out, teachers and staff gathered to discuss how to deal with the aftermath, but Mr. Pan and Mr. Li were still in bed. Students filled the school with declarations and slogans within half an hour of the upheaval, indicating that they had prepared in advance. Mr. Pan and Mr. Li were in charge of discipline and dormitory affairs, so why did they have no precautions and why did they behave ambiguously after the fact, as if they were indifferent? Moreover, they told the school principal that students had not overstepped their bounds and had no background. From the perspective of the party, they did not feel that there was any violation. The best solution now is to fully accommodate the students' demands. Subsequently, the principal lectured repeatedly, and the teachers and staff repeatedly persuaded, but Mr. Pan and others never said a word. This is the real situation before and after the upheaval. After the upheaval broke out, the school principal, seeing that the relationship between Director Dai and the students had broken down, approved Director Dai's resignation. Then, the students' goal had been achieved, and it seemed that they should resume classes immediately. However, the students became even more arrogant, rushing to the undergraduate department to disrupt order on the 1st, and obstructing the undergraduate memorial week and beating the undergraduate dormitory staff member Zhu Zhihua on the 3rd. Their actions became increasingly absurd. On the 4th, they received a telegram from the Ministry of Education ordering a thorough investigation and proper handling to maintain academic discipline. Therefore, the principal convened a school affairs meeting to discuss solutions. After a four-hour meeting, it was unanimously agreed that the students who led the beating of teachers, held hostage, and boycotted classes were defying the law and beyond the reach of school education. Only by selecting and punishing them could academic discipline be maintained. Therefore, on the morning of the 5th, the leading troublemakers, Sun Cuifu, Zang Zhongchun, Jing Zhichang, Xiang Xuehai, Zhang Da, Zhou Jun, Shen Ruilin, Wu Xixiang, Zhao Chuanxu, Sheng Hua, He Senni, Zhang Shu, Zhou Zhiang, Zeng Yuanpei, Wang Hanxiong, and other fifteen students were expelled and escorted out of the campus. Those whose circumstances were lighter were given demerits, including Wu Tingchen, Pan Xikang, Li Hongxun, Hua Younian, Song Fengzhai, Chu Fusheng, Zhu Jingyuan, Xu Zhengshi, Jin Fa, Ye Haoquan, Zhang Hancai, Shao Jinpeng, Jiang Yintang, Wang Qinghao, Fu Zhengfu, Zhang Guoji, Zhao Peishou, Fang Zhenzhong, Xie Jingyuan, Yang Bosong, and other twenty people. At that time, Mr. Pan, who instigated the upheaval, had abandoned his post and left the school on the afternoon of the 3rd. Therefore, the students no longer insisted and signed their names, willing to resume classes immediately. Therefore, the order was restored from 10:00 a.m., and students who left the school have been notified to return to school by newspaper and letter. This is the real situation of handling the upheaval.

Fortunately, the current upheaval has been quelled with the assistance of party headquarters at all levels and local agencies, as well as the upholding of public opinion by the media. On the 5th, a lecture was convened, and classes were resumed as usual. On the morning of the 6th, Secretary Huang Shaohong, a representative of the Ministry of Education, came to the school to earnestly lecture the students. The students expressed their remorse on the spot, saying that they would never overstep their bounds again. Therefore, the upheaval was completely resolved. However, after the pain subsides, thinking about the endless disturbances and the days of students' time and studies being unnecessarily sacrificed, the minority's conspiracy to trap the whole situation in destruction fills the heart with unspeakable guilt. Respectfully summarizing the main points and sincerely reporting them, I humbly request your judgment.

Furthermore, it is reported that Secretary Huang Shaohong was previously sent by the provincial government to Suzhou to investigate and believed that the school's handling of the upheaval was extremely appropriate. The previous evening, the Provincial Party Affairs Reorganization Committee sent Comrade Song Yufeng to Suzhou to investigate. Yesterday afternoon, accompanied by Mr. Yan and Mr. Jiang from the County Party Headquarters, they went to the school for a detailed six-hour investigation, believing that Pan Tianjue was indeed suspected of instigating the upheaval and will report the findings to the province for review.

Refusal of Song Binggong by Education Sector in Fengxian, Via Telegram 91

Since the provincial government's 345th meeting appointed Song Binggong as the director of the Fengxian County Education Bureau, the entire county's education sector has been outraged and unanimously opposed. The telegram to the provincial government is recorded below:

Submitted for Review: It was recently reported with shock and dismay that the provincial government meeting has approved the appointment of Song Binggong to replace Zhan Song as the director of the County Education Bureau. The entire sector is bewildered. Article 17 of the revised County Organization Law promulgated by the National Government in July of this year stipulates that each bureau of the county government shall have one director, to be selected by the county magistrate from among qualified candidates who have passed the examination and submitted to the provincial government for approval. If there is a real need to change the director of the County Education Bureau, it should be handled in accordance with the law. However, the provincial government directly appointed him without going through the county magistrate's selection process, which means that the promulgated County Organization Law is not being treated as a mere formality. Moreover, it is heard that Song Binggong is affiliated with Nantong and is completely unfamiliar with the situation in the county. It is inappropriate for him to come to lead education as the people and place are not suitable. The county does not lack qualified personnel, so why borrow talent from other places? The sector believes that the issue of the director's selection is of great importance to the future of education and in order to respect the law, it is impossible to recognize the education director who has not been produced in accordance with the County Organization Law. We especially request the Honorable Department to investigate and promptly forward this to the provincial government to withdraw the appointment and order the Fengxian County government to select and submit a candidate for approval in accordance with the law, so as to comply with the law and emphasize education. We are awaiting orders with extreme urgency. Respectfully submitted to Chen, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Education Department.

Sports

Westerners' Football Club Middle Group Competition 96

Zhenru Lost to Shanghai

Two to Three :: First Half One to One

The Westerners' Club Group A Championship match between the Zhenru Football Team and the Shanghai Westerners' Team was held at Shen Garden yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM. After ninety minutes of fierce fighting, Zhenru lost 2-3. The referee was Maxwell, and the linesmen were Liang Guocai for Zhenru and Irwin for Shanghai.

Inconvenience of Marching in the Mud 97

Due to continuous heavy rain, the roads are muddy and all the football fields have become swamps. The athletes' football shoes are hung high, suffering from being unable to display their skills. Fortunately, the weather cleared up yesterday, and the game was held. However, the green field was saturated with water, and it was difficult to run, with falls and tumbles occurring at any time. The ball became heavier and harder to use. The Westerners had strong physical strength and occupied a lot of ground. However, after being exhausted in battle, they were not as agile as the Chinese.

No Hope of Victory Without the Center Forward 98

Zhenru's strength is not below that of Shanghai. Initially, they were troubled by not being good at fighting in wet conditions, but after a long time, they gained the essence of it and saw themselves on par, with a fierce aggression that was astonishing. But heaven did not bless Zhenru, causing their main forward general Dai Linjing to be injured and unable to play. Otherwise, the outcome of the victory or defeat would not be predictable. Chen Zhenhe is the bravest of the three armies, a versatile talent on the football field. He can still be considered competent in defense, but the forward connection is not pure, and the inside and outside cannot communicate in one breath, which is his major problem. The most outstanding talent in the Shanghai team is the left inside forward Cole. The performance of the left winger Henry is also good. Inside players Stoke and Monroe can also be active and productive. The victory came mostly from hand-to-hand combat, as they can make good use of their innate physical strength.

(3) The Lineup of the Two Teams 99

Shanghai Team: Gray Rook, Stoke, Fabin, Sumner, Monroe, Sheffer, Henry, Cole, Sinclair, Bowden, Bright

Zhenru Team: Liang Guanlian, Feng Yunyou, Jiang Shanjing, Lin Songfa, Chen Zhenhe, Zhuang Shihong, Chen Bingxiang, Fu Hexuan, Dai Linjing, Chen Jiaqiu, Mei Hongbao

(4) A Misstep Almost Became an Eternal Regret 100

The bell rang three times, and the battle began. Shanghai rushed in like a tide, and a dangerous situation immediately appeared. The left winger Henry passed the ball accurately, and center forward Sinclair advanced quickly, but the goalkeeper rushed out to save and they stumbled and fell to the ground, narrowly missing the goal. The momentum reversed, and Dai charged straight in. Suddenly, he passed to the right to Mei, who quickly picked up the ball, and the enemy formation became chaotic. Fu leaped forward to meet the ball, but was unable to stop in time, and his full of hope turned into smoke. Shanghai's right wing rose up again, and the hand-to-hand combat gradually approached the hinterland. Goalkeeper Liang looked flustered and did not know what to do. A ball from the right went through the empty goal, and the right winger Henry kicked it with a thunderous applause, seeming to predict its success, but the ball did not follow his heart and flew high.

(5) Each Side Scored a Goal in Ten Minutes 101

Shanghai continued to attack with strong momentum. Bowden made a horizontal attack, and the ball happened to be intercepted by Chen Zhenhe, who was offside, and it rolled into the goal. It was truly a case of "shooting oneself in the foot." After conceding a goal, Zhenru tried to recover, and the five forwards used low and near passes, advancing step by step. When they reached the city, the left and right encirclement had formed. Although the enemy was stubborn, they felt it difficult to take care of both sides. In the moment of decision, the goalkeeper saved the ball and fell to the ground, and Fu Hexuan touched the ground and rolled into the net. Both sides scored a goal, with the time before and after being within ten minutes. After this fifteen minutes, the strength was equal and it was difficult to distinguish the victory or defeat. The first half ended with a score of one to one.

(6) Lost the Goal Again and the General Was Injured 102

The whistle blew, and the Shanghai team advanced in five ways with unstoppable momentum. Zhenru's front and rear defense lines were lost. The enemy filled the front of the goal and fought to the death without retreating. Finally, Henry received Bowden's ball and shot it into the goal while falling to the ground. At that time, Dai was leading the forwards to counterattack and the situation was serious, but he suffered an injury to his leg and it was difficult to move, so he had to leave the field for rest. Since then, Zhenru lacked a general, and the strength of the eleven against ten was not as good as before. Chen Zhenhe held the important position of the center back and always took the lead in battle. Once, he took advantage of the enemy's emptiness to directly attack the goal, but after a moment of hesitation, he was pushed out by the goalkeeper.

(7) Outnumbered and Outflanked 103

Five minutes later, Chen Zhenhe executed a free kick 30 yards from the goal, and the ball went straight into the enemy's goal and over the goal, missing by only an inch. Shanghai Stoke kicked a free kick in the center of the field and landed in front of the goal. Cole crossed arms with Zhu of Chen Bingxiang and made a surprising move, carrying the ball out of his own formation and rushing all the way without any obstacles. Unexpectedly, the two inside defenders of Shanghai chased from behind to stop him and prevent him from kicking, and the whole effort was in vain. In the blink of an eye, Shanghai launched another attack on the goal, and Bowden passed a ball horizontally. Cole calmly shot and Shanghai took a 3-1 lead.

(8) Showing Skills and Winning Back a Goal 104

In this critical situation, Zhenru used all its strength, and although they were at a disadvantage, their offense was stronger than the enemy's. Chen Zhenhe tried his best in the front and was quite active. At 4:25, Mei Hongbao passed from the right to the middle, Chen Zhenhe chased and collided with the goalkeeper and fell to the ground. The ball rebounded and Mei kicked it into the empty goal, making it 2-3. Zhenru was still behind by one goal. At this time, Shanghai's situation was reversed and became dangerous. The injured goalkeeper could not perform his duties and was replaced by Sinclair. Zhenru completely went from being attacked to being in the position of attacking. Shanghai could only retreat completely to maintain the winning situation. When the goalkeeper came out again, it was difficult for Shanghai to restore its military appearance. As a result, Shanghai still won 3-2, which can be said to be fortunate.

The center forward Zhang Guanxiang took the ball and directly attacked the enemy alone. He turned over and kicked it accurately. In the first half, First Song won two goals. In the second half, Health held the determination to break the boat and attacked desperately, rushing horizontally and vertically like a swift wind and rain, and the ball often wandered within the First Song position. Relying on the central defender Du Renlin and the left guard Lin Shouye to resist, although the dangerous situation was endless, they finally maintained their defense and still won the final victory with a score of 2-0.
